# Hamnix STATUS — milestone log

The full milestone trajectory across three tracks: the bare-metal Hamnix
kernel (M-series), the Linux ABI compatibility track (L-series), and the
Linux userspace ABI track (U-series).

**Status legend:**
- **Done** — landed on `main` with a passing test.
- **Partial** — landed but a documented gap remains.
- **Diagnosis** — investigated, documented blocker, no code change.
- **Pending** — not yet started.

For the current end-state plus open blockers, see [README.md](README.md).
For docs/architecture spec, see [docs/architecture.md](docs/architecture.md).
For agent-orchestrated development workflow, see [README.md§Agent-orchestrated development](README.md#agent-orchestrated-development).

> **Current boot model (read this before the milestone log below).**
> There is **no pre-baked root disk image** anymore. The single install
> artifact is `build/hamnix-installer.img` (built by
> `scripts/build_installer_img.sh`) — an ESP-only **UEFI-only** GPT image
> whose kernel + embedded squashfs root are loaded entirely into RAM by
> firmware; the in-RAM installer then partitions the target's NVMe and
> writes a persistent **GPT + ESP + ext4 root**, then reboots off that
> disk alone. The installed system boots when UEFI launches the native
> PE/COFF stub off the NVMe ESP, which ELF-loads `\hamnix-kernel.elf`;
> the kernel finds the ext4 root via its `.hamnix-roots` sentinel, binds
> `#sysroot` at `/`, and ELF-loads `/init` off ext4. For VM testing,
> `scripts/build_installed_nvme.sh` runs that real installer path once
> into a golden disk `build/hamnix-installed.qcow2`, and feature tests
> boot a fresh copy via `scripts/_installed_boot.sh`. **There is no
> BIOS/legacy/CSM path, no GRUB, and no bootable ISO** —
> `scripts/build_iso.sh` is now a shim that delegates to
> `build_installer_img.sh`. The in-kernel cpio initramfs is retained for
> the developer `-kernel` test path and as the installer's in-RAM root.
> Many milestone rows below are date-stamped historical records of the
> earlier hybrid-ISO / baked-image model and are preserved as history,
> not current state.

---

## Status

| Milestone | Description | Status |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| T3 | **Self-hosting compiler cutover** — the native `.ad` host compiler (`build/cutover/host_ac.elf`) is now the **DEFAULT** build compiler (`scripts/_adder_cc.sh` ADDER_CC=adder). Builds the whole kernel + all userland; installer image behaviorally identical to the Python seed (fuzzer 500/500; userland objdiff 193 clean; new kernel objdiff 0 collisions/0 divergences across 10162 funcs; native rl5 PASS + desktop visually verified). ~300x faster per-compile. Python seed = frozen bootstrap + oracle only. | **Done** |
| T4 | **Native-in-Adder optimizer Phases 1–3** — IR scaffold + pass manager + constant-folding (P1), local CSE/value-numbering (P2), LICM (P3), all in `adder/compiler/{ir,opt}.ad`. OPT-IN behind `ADDER_OPT=1`/`--opt`, **DEFAULT OFF** (default codegen stays byte-identical to seed: all 3 differentials green). Fuzzer ADDER_OPT=1 correctness lane. Phase 4 (regalloc, needs whole-function CFG IR + liveness) is the next big win. | **Partial** |
| T5 | **SMP scheduler concurrency hardening** — fixed the `-kernel -smp 2` boot-first-task steal race (PID 1 published STATE_EMBRYO until `start_first_task` claims it; `test_hamsh_heartbeat` green), then landed the `on_cpu` handshake + reap fence + AP CPL3-dispatch fix so **user tasks load-balance across CPUs** (`test_smp_user` PASS). Closes the #413 steal-window family. | **Done** |
| T6 | **Linux-ABI windowed-mmap reclaim** — `mm/vma.ad` per-task free-list reclaims freed 4-MiB `[1G,4G)` window VAs so apt's large `.so` closure stops exhausting the window (was `-ENOMEM` → ld.so 'failed to map segment'). Compile + boot verified; apt-install e2e gated on the debian fixture. | **Partial** |
| T7 | **Self-hosting cutover 100% COMPLETE** — `host_ac` now compiles the ENTIRE kernel (kobjdiff 0 divergences / 10211 funcs) AND all 213 userland units natively — ZERO Python-seed fallback. Closers: un-reserve `bytes`/`field` lexer keywords (restored native kernel build) + 3 codegen.ad gaps (string-literal index, function-pointer value, `sys_waitpid`/`sys_pgrp_kill` wrappers) closing the last 16 userland units. | **Done** |
| T8 | **Native optimizer Phase 4 — register allocation** — whole-function CFG + per-block liveness + value-level live ranges + alias/clobber analysis (`adder/compiler/cfg.ad`), then a linear-scan allocator (`regalloc.ad`) over callee-saved regs (call-crossing free), annotation form. OPT-IN behind `ADDER_OPT`, DEFAULT OFF (byte-inert; 3 differentials green); correctness lane 500/500 + register-pressure corpus. Full IR-consuming backend is the remaining speedup. | **Partial** |
| T9 | **DE OOM/panel fix (user-reported)** — every hamui app baked 8.2 MB of static framebuffer BSS; the ELF loader eagerly contiguous-allocated it per app → `elf: OOM` crash + no panel under `-m 1G`. Fixed by demand-paging the ELF64 BSS tail (`fs/elf.ad`) + right-sizing hamui backbuffers to the actual window via demand-zero mmap (`lib/hamui.ad`, ~8 MB→<1 MB/app). Crash + panel fixed, VISUALLY verified 3 boots. (Residual: desktop-icons/cursor-ghost flaky under extreme host load.) | **Done** |
| T10 | **SMAP/SMEP kernel-image protection** — the kernel high-half (.text/.rodata/.data/.bss + module window) was stamped US=1 (CPL3-readable) and the US=0 restamp was gated on `smap_supported` (never ran on non-KVM). Now unconditional US=0 restamp at the creation layer + US=0 module map; audit reports 0 high-half US=1 leaks; SMAP-enforcement test (user read of kernel VA faults) PASS. Unblocks KASLR/KPTI. | **Done** |
| T11 | **DE live-image OOM regression FIX (user-reported, orchestrator-VISUALLY-verified)** — the default installer image's in-RAM live distro had grown to **361 MiB** (the full real-Debian apt/dpkg closure was staged into the RAM image by default), but only ~316 MiB is free under the user's `-m 1G` ship command → `[live-root] memblock_alloc(378535936) failed`, the rootfs half-loaded, and the DE OOM'd spawning apps (bare teal desktop). Fix: the live in-RAM distro now defaults to a **minimal busybox namespace** (`HAMNIX_LIVE_MINIMAL`, build_rootfs_img.py / build_installer_img.sh) — 361→55 MiB; the heavy apt closure moves to the persistent installed disk / opt-in flag (apt-e2e image sets `HAMNIX_LIVE_MINIMAL=0`). Full desktop (panel + 3 app windows) boots clean at `-m 1G`, 0 OOM — orchestrator viewed the screendump. (Supersedes the T9 hamui-backbuffer fix, which is in-tree but was not the live-image regression.) | **Done** |
| T15 | **Linux-namespace apt/dpkg KEYSTONE — `dpkg -i` completes** — the fork+exec COW-isolation bug is fixed (`_cow_share_one_page` refcounts verbatim-RO shared mmap frames so a child's exec/reap teardown no longer frees a frame the parent still maps) + a cascade of install-pipeline ABI fills (rmdir/rename/lseek-ESPIPE/utimensat/O_TRUNC/*at-anchoring/binfmt_script/EFER.NXE-per-CPU). `dpkg -i` now reaches "Setting up hamhello" + the installed binary runs; all 3 gates (apt-e2e, heartbeat, dynamic_forkexec) green. `enter linux {sh}` is interactive over a real Debian root. | **Done** |
| T17 | **DE memory footprint −21 MiB + hamsh lexer truncation fix** — hamUId compositor BSS 40→20 MiB (DMAX 32→12, SCENE_CACHE right-sized, wallpaper buffers demand-mmap'd); DE boots full (panel+apps) with ~372 MiB free of 842 under `-m 1G`, zero OOM (orchestrator-VISUALLY verified). CRITICAL latent fix: hamsh's lexer silently truncated past `TOK_MAX=512`, so once `rc.5` grew past it the script truncated → parse error → BLANK desktop; now `TOK_MAX=4096` + all 6 token arrays resized + loud overflow error + CI guards (`test_hamsh_tok_capacity.sh`). Heartbeat green (clean host). | **Done** |
| T20 | **DE-OOM regression FIX + user-reported bug wave** — (1) a coverage agent un-gated-embedded ~120 Debian binaries into the DEFAULT installer cpio, bloating it 214→297 MiB → DE OOM on `-m 1G` (blank/partial desktop). Gated behind `HAMNIX_DEBIAN_BREADTH`; image back to 216 MiB; added `test_installer_img_size.sh` (fail >260 MiB) as a RAM-independent bloat tripwire; DE-tests default to 2G RAM (`HAMNIX_VM_MEM`). (2) A userspace process fault (the user's `ls \| grep`) was HALTING the kernel via the ring3-bringup trap-diag handler — now a CPL3 read-prot #PF delivers SIGSEGV+coredump+reap and the kernel keeps running (`test_user_fault_survivable` PASS). (3) hamedit Ctrl-S now persists saves + surfaces read-only write failures honestly. (4) Ops: reclaimed ~321 GB by pruning 1060 stale agent worktrees. All orchestrator-VISUALLY verified (full desktop at -m 1G, 216 MiB). | **Done** |
| T18b | **Optimizer — regalloc on the IR (scratch-register pool)** — the IR emit path now parks binop operands in callee-saved scratch registers (drawn from the linear-scan pool not claimed by a promoted local, provably disjoint, call-crossing-safe) instead of `%rbp` stack slots: 7→0 push/pop pairs on the register-pressure benchmark. Also FOUND+FIXED a pre-existing regalloc miscompile (≥7-param stack-arg read at the wrong `%rbp` offset when callee-saved regs are pushed). Flag-off objdiff 210/210 byte-clean; flag-on 800/800 correct + call-crossing/spill corpus. | **Done** |
| T18 | **Native optimizer Phase 6/7 — IR coverage 4%→87% + cross-statement CSE** — IR-consuming backend broadened to compares + div/mod/shr + cast/index leaves (~87% of binary-op roots), then cross-statement CSE on extended basic blocks (redundant subexpr across statements eliminated, with conservative aliasing-store invalidation + LICM zero-trip/trap safety). Hot loop 4081→3514 dynamic instrs (13.9% fewer), seed-identical. Flag-off objdiff 210/210 byte-clean; flag-on 800/800 correct + aliasing/LICM-safety corpus. | **Done** |
| T19 | **`apt-get install` from a local repo (Linux-ns)** — staged the dpkg CPU/arch tables + `/etc/apt/apt.conf.d` that apt-get's config-dir read + architecture detection needed (the "Unable to read apt.conf.d" / "Error reading the CPU table" blockers); apt-get install driven from a local file:// repo. Complements the `dpkg -i` keystone (T15). apt-e2e gate confirmation in progress. | **Partial** |
| T16 | **`enter linux {sh}` interactive crash FIX + DE UX fixes (user-reported)** — interactive dash crashed on the first forked command: the signal trampoline lives in kernel `.text` (stamped US=0 by the T10 SMAP hardening), so a SIGCHLD-handler's CPL3 trampoline fetch NX-faulted; fixed by mapping it US=1 RO+X per Linux task (vDSO-style) + a signal-frame RSP fix. Verified (interactive-dash + heartbeat + dynamic_forkexec green). DE UX: hamedit now opens the file passed to it (argv), new windows auto-raise+focus (z-order, devwsys), terminal arrow-keys do history + inline editing — orchestrator-VISUALLY verified (terminal raised topmost, live shell). | **Done** |
| T13 | **Native optimizer Phase 5 — genuine IR-consuming emit backend** — pure signedness-invariant integer arithmetic subtrees now lower AST→IR→optimize→emit (`gen_expr_ir`/`try_gen_expr_ir` in codegen.ad over opt.ad's IR), with constant-tail reassociation (`(a+3)+4→a+7`) the AST pass can't do; everything else falls back to the AST emitter. Found+fixed a float-guard bug en route. OPT-IN behind `ADDER_OPT`, DEFAULT OFF byte-identical (objdiff 210/210 clean, 500/500 off-lane); flag-on 700/700 correct, 0 miscompiles; 100% of a 120-prog corpus exercised the IR path. Also: methods (`gen_method`) now register-promote (T8 extension). | **Partial** |
| T14 | **Cross-process COW physical-RAM aliasing FIX** — the boot stub identity-maps low 512 GiB with PRESENT US=0 1 GiB huge pages, so >4 GiB ASLR windows (ET_DYN/interp/mmap) were a present phys==vaddr stamp; cracking them (`_build_pd_from_pdpt_entry`/`_build_pt_from_pd_entry`) reproduced identity sub-leaves that aliased the SAME physical RAM into every process using that window → a fork child's exec could scribble the parent's live image. Fixed (`fs/elf.ad` `_is_boot_identity_stamp` guard → seed EMPTY leaves for present identity stamps above RAM top). Heartbeat 1158 ticks + full build + DE desktop (orchestrator-viewed) all green. Unblocks a chunk of the Linux-ns fork/exec path; one apt fork+exec COW-isolation residual remains (characterized). | **Done** |
| T21 | **User hands-on bug wave (in flight) + optimizer floats** — LANDED (local main, push held behind the DE visual gate): (a) **float arithmetic into the IR optimizer** — `+,-,*,/` + compares lower AST→IR→SSE (`addsd/mulsd`/`ss` variants, mixed-precision converts); flag-off objdiff **210/210 byte-clean**, flag-on fuzzer-correct, IR-root coverage 86.8→94.6%. (b) **apt-get** dpkg-table/`apt.conf.d` cpio staging + a **W^X shared-page false-SIGSEGV fix** (`fs/elf.ad`: a non-page-aligned RO PT_LOAD shares its last page with the next RW segment; the RO flip dragged the shared writable page read-only). (c) **MATE-parity panels** — config-driven `hampanelscene` (top+bottom + per-edge L/R, vertical-layout cut-off fix, right-click Add/Move/Remove, `/etc/panel.conf` persistence) + terminal default-size fix; DE structural guards retargeted off the retired `hampanel`/`hambottom`. **fork keystone DONE+pushed** (`32ae348c`): the user's `ls \| grep` "can't fork: EAGAIN" + the pipeline-hang were ONE root cause — the SMP buddy page allocator (`mm/page_alloc.ad`) had NO cross-CPU lock, so a spawn/reap-heavy pipeline raced the free-list splices on two CPUs → either a `_try_remove_buddy` spin-with-IRQs-masked whole-box freeze or `alloc_pages`→0 at fork (= the EAGAIN); fixed with an IRQ-safe buddy spinlock + bounded pipe EOF wait. The glibc `__libc_fork`/`_dl_stack_used` SIGSEGV was already cured by the W^X clip (`388b0e51`). Gates: `test_u37_busybox_pipe3` PASS+XPASS, `test_dynamic_forkexec` PASS, SMP heartbeat 1088 ticks, DE visually verified. STAGED (local, push held for quiet re-verify): serial `enter linux {sh}` interactive (kernel `/dev/cons` UART read was foreground-gated → DE-owned-foreground starved a serial-spawned linux sh; now grab-gated only) + `newshell hostowner` uid-1 self-elevation w/o password (`3cba2938`; serial-#1 test PASS + DE visual PASS, hostowner/heartbeat gates flaked under concurrent fuzzer load). | **Partial** |
| T12 | **KASLR v2 — per-boot kernel-window randomization** — `kaslr_offset` is now a real non-zero per-boot value (RDRAND/RDTSC entropy via `arch_get_random_u64`) that 2 MiB-granularly slides the module-mapping-window base (where loaded `.ko` `.text`/`.rodata`/`.data` land — the classic KASLR target). Three boots → distinct offsets; heartbeat SMP gate green. Static kernel-image base (`-no-pie`, baked absolutes) is still fixed — full-image relocation is the v3 follow-up. | **Done** |

| M16.93 | Phase B: Plan 9 syscall numbers reserved + SYS_ERRSTR (265). 9 new numbers stubbed (-ENOSYS): rfork (256), bind (257), mount (258), unmount (259), create (260), stat (261), fstat (262), remove (263), fd2path (264). SYS_ERRSTR has a real body in `sys/src/9/port/error.ad` with 9front-style swap-buffer semantics; reads the per-task `errstr_buf` (128 B inline in `TaskStruct`) into a user buffer, and if the user buffer carries a non-empty string, installs that as the new current error. Integrated at exactly one failure path (SYS_OPEN → -ENOENT installs "file does not exist") so `tests/test_errstr.ad` can round-trip the message end-to-end. Foundation for every following Plan 9 native syscall — they all need `errstr` to report errors. | M16.94 | Plan 9 `/dev/cons` device file — `vfs_open('/dev/cons')` (and the OWRITE variant) returns an `FD_CONS_MARK` fd whose read side blocks on the existing kbd/UART RX FIFOs and whose write side fans bytes through `early_putc()` to UART + VGA/fb + printk. | M16.95 | Plan 9 `/dev/time` + `/dev/pid` + `/dev/random` device files — three new stateless cdevs under `sys/src/9/port/devtime.ad`, `devpid.ad`, `devrandom.ad` with `FD_TIME_MARK` (0xFFFFFFF0) / `FD_PID_MARK` (0xFFFFFFEF) / `FD_RANDOM_MARK` (0xFFFFFFEE) plumbing in `fs/vfs.ad`. `/dev/time` reads emit `get_jiffies()*10_000_000` ns-since-boot as ASCII decimal + `\n` (HZ=100 → 10 ms per tick); `/dev/pid` reads emit `current_task_pid()` as ASCII decimal + `\n`; `/dev/random` reads stream xorshift64 bytes (lazy-seeded from `get_jiffies()` mixed with the golden-ratio constant on first read — placeholder pending chacha20 + RDRAND/RDSEED). Writes return -1 on time/pid; `/dev/random` XOR-folds writes into the PRNG state as entropy mix. Retires the `SYS_GET_JIFFIES → read("/dev/time")` and `SYS_GETPID → read("/dev/pid")` rows in the migration table. See `scripts/test_devtime.sh`, `scripts/test_devpid.sh`, `scripts/test_devrandom.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.96 | DHCP client + virtio_net_tx public surface + IPv4/UDP/ICMP scaffold (`drivers/net/dhcp.ad`, `drivers/net/ip.ad`, `drivers/net/udp.ad`, `drivers/net/icmp.ad`, `drivers/net/virtio_net.ad` +`virtio_net_tx`). `eth_tx()` now wires through to the TX virtqueue (replaces the M16.90 log-and-drop stub); `ip_send()` builds the 20-byte IPv4 header with Internet checksum and resolves dst MAC via the ARP cache (broadcast for `255.255.255.255`, gateway MAC for off-subnet). DHCP client runs the four-way DISCOVER → OFFER → REQUEST → ACK handshake against SLIRP, captures `10.0.2.15` + gateway `10.0.2.2`, and mirrors them into the IP layer + ARP responder. ICMP echo request/reply skeleton lands but the reply parse path is gated by an arp_lookup codegen quirk fixed in M16.97. See `scripts/test_net_dhcp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.97 | ICMP echo round-trip — finishes the M16.96 scaffold. Root cause was two Adder codegen quirks in `arp_lookup`: (1) `cast[uint64](arp_ip[i])` on an `Array[N, uint32]` global doesn't zero-extend cleanly across `==`, so the equality compare reported "not equal" even when bit-patterns matched; (2) `&arp_mac[i][0]` on the 2-D `Array[N, Array[6, uint8]]` MAC table lowered to address 0 instead of the correct slot, so `ip_send` saw `dst_mac == NULL` and dropped every outbound IP frame. Workaround in `drivers/net/arp.ad`: load `arp_ip[i]` through an explicit `Ptr[uint32]` + mask, and offset off `&arp_mac` arithmetically (`mac_base + i*6`). Both quirks documented in `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` for a future compiler milestone. With the fix, `[icmp] echo request -> 10.0.2.2` followed by `[icmp] echo reply from 10.0.2.2` round-trips through the SLIRP gateway — first proof of two-way IPv4 in the bare-metal kernel. See `scripts/test_net_icmp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.98 | Phase C: Plan 9 `rfork(2)` (SYS_RFORK = 256) lands its real body in `sys/src/9/port/sysproc.ad`, replacing the M16.93 -ENOSYS stub. POSIX-fork combo `rfork(RFPROC \| RFFDG \| RFNAMEG \| RFENVG)` creates a new task that returns the child pid in the parent and 0 in the child; in-place mutation (no RFPROC) privatises the namespace via RFNAMEG / RFCNAMEG. `TaskStruct` grows three sharing-state fields (`fd_table_refcount`, `namespace_id`, `note_group`) with matching accessors + monotonic id allocators (`alloc_namespace_id` / `alloc_note_group_id`) in `kernel/sched/core.ad`. `user/runtime.S` adds a `sys_rfork(flags)` wrapper that stashes the parent's user-side `%rbp` into syscall arg a5 so `do_rfork` can patch the child's initial `__switch_to` stack image (without this the child's first RBP-relative local read after rfork lands on the parent's stack page). `RFMEM` (thread path) returns -ENOSYS in this commit — full thread route lands in a follow-up. SYS_CLONE (3) stays untouched for the Linux ABI; both work concurrently. See `scripts/test_rfork.sh` for the end-to-end fixture. Cornerstone of the Plan 9-shape process control surface — replaces fork / vfork / clone / pthread_create / unshare with one flag-bit primitive | **Done** |
| M16.99 | Minimal DNS resolver client (`drivers/net/dns.ad`) — UDP/53 A-record queries against the DHCP-supplied DNS server (option 6, captured by `dhcp_get_dns` added to `drivers/net/dhcp.ad`). `dns_lookup("example.com", out_ip, timeout)` is the synchronous entry point: it primes the ARP cache with a one-shot REQUEST for the DNS server (10.0.2.3 under SLIRP has its own MAC distinct from the gateway at 10.0.2.2, so the M16.88 probe doesn't cover it), builds a 12-byte header + length-prefixed QNAME + QTYPE=A/QCLASS=IN, sends from an ephemeral source port in the 53000..53003 pool, and polls `virtio_net_poll()` until `dns_rx` flips the slot to "answered" or the deadline elapses. Response parser walks past the question section (honoring 0xC0-0xC0 compression pointers) and scans the answer section for the first A-record's RDATA. 4-slot in-flight table dodges the M16.97 2-D-array-address codegen quirk by flattening per-slot result bytes into a 1-D `Array[16, uint8]`. `udp_rx` dispatches dst-port 53000..53003 → `dns_rx`. `[dns] resolved example.com -> 172.66.147.243` against QEMU SLIRP's DNS forwarder is the proof-of-life marker; test accepts `[dns] timeout` as a SKIP for sandboxed CI without internet. See `scripts/test_dns.sh`. Unblocks `apt update http://deb.debian.org` reaching real package mirrors by name | **Done** |
| M16.100 | PS/2 keyboard polish for real-hardware install console (`drivers/input/atkbd.ad`). Extends the M16.75 Set-1 scaffold with: extended-scancode handling via a sticky `in_e0_prefix` flag (arrow keys, Home/End, Insert/Delete, PageUp/Down, right Ctrl, right Alt/AltGr); modifier-state bitmask (`MOD_SHIFT`/`CTRL`/`ALT`/`CAPS`/`NUM`) driven by make/break for Shift/Ctrl/Alt and toggle-on-make-only for CapsLock/NumLock; Shift+letter and Caps+letter folded via XOR (both pressed cancels, matching every PC keyboard since 1985); Shift+symbol routed through a parallel `sc1_to_shifted` table (`1`→`!`, ``` ` ```→`~`, …, US-104 layout); Ctrl+letter folded to 0x01..0x1A via `& 0x1F` so Ctrl-C still produces 0x03 and the M16.42 SIGINT path keeps working; F1..F4 emit VT220 SS3 escapes (`ESC O P/Q/R/S`), F5..F12 + Insert/Delete/PageUp/PageDown emit `ESC [ <digits> ~`, arrows emit `ESC [ A/B/C/D`. Boot-time `atkbd_self_test()` feeds 12 synthetic scancode sequences through `atkbd_process_byte()` and asserts 25 FIFO bytes; banner `atkbd: self-test PASS (25 cases)` is the regression criterion in `scripts/test_atkbd_ext.sh`. | M16.101 | Phase C: Plan 9 file-operations cluster — `create` (260), `stat` (261), `fstat` (262), `remove` (263), `fd2path` (264) — real bodies in `sys/src/9/port/sysfile.ad`, replacing the M16.93 -ENOSYS stubs. `do_create` delegates to `vfs_open_write`; DMDIR returns -1 + errstr "create failed: DMDIR not supported" (no `vfs_mkdir` backend yet). `do_stat` walks the cpio archive and serialises a 9P-shape `Dir` record per `docs/native-api.md`'s "Directory format". `do_fstat` handles per-`FD_*_MARK` synthetic dirs (cons / time / pid / random / null / zero / stdin / stdout / stderr / dir / pipe) plus initramfs fds. `do_remove` is a thin `vfs_unlink` wrapper. `do_fd2path` returns canonical cpio name for initramfs fds (best-effort; per-fd path slot deferred to Phase G). `user/runtime.S` gains a generic `syscall6(nr, a0..a5)` trampoline. | M16.102 | Minimal TCP/IPv4 client (active-open only) in `drivers/net/tcp.ad` — fleshes out the M16.51 scaffold into a real state machine. 8-entry static TCB table (parallel arrays, slot-index = ephemeral-port-offset from 50000), states CLOSED → SYN_SENT → ESTABLISHED → FIN_WAIT_1/2 → TIME_WAIT → CLOSED (passive-open / LISTEN deferred until sshd needs it). Public API: `tcp_connect(ip4, port, timeout)` returns slot; `tcp_send(slot, buf, len)` writes one segment + polls for ACK; `tcp_recv(slot, buf, max, timeout)` polls until data lands; `tcp_close(slot)` runs the FIN/ACK/FIN/ACK termination. ISN xorshift64-seeded off `get_jiffies()`. Checksum builds the IPv4 pseudo-header (src_ip + dst_ip + 0 + proto=6 + tcp_length) into a scratch prefix before the segment and feeds the whole thing through `ip_csum16` — same algorithm UDP/ICMP use, just with a different prefix. `ip_rx` gains a `proto == 6` dispatch path to `tcp_rx`. **Real bug found**: `ip_rx` previously handed the L4 demuxer the full buffer length, so a 40-byte TCP-ACK delivered in a 60-byte Ethernet-padded frame looked like it carried 6 bytes of phantom payload, advancing `rcv_nxt` past the next real data and dropping the echo; the fix trusts the IPv4 `total_length` field (capped at buffer length to defend against spoofed sizes). On-link destinations are ARP-primed via a one-shot REQUEST before the SYN; off-link targets route via the M16.96 gateway MAC. Smoke test in `init/main.ad:tcp_smoke_test` opens to 10.0.2.100:7 (SLIRP `guestfwd=tcp:10.0.2.100:7-cmd:cat` echoes via the host's `cat`), sends `"hi\n"`, reads it back, closes. Markers `[tcp] connected slot=0` / `[tcp] sent 3 bytes` / `[tcp] received 3 bytes: 'hi\n'` / `[tcp] closed slot=0` are the PASS criteria. No retransmission, no congestion control beyond cwnd=1 segment, no SACK / timestamps / window scaling (all explicitly out of scope for SLIRP's loss-free virtual wire). Unblocks the HTTP client that `apt update` needs. See `scripts/test_net_tcp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.103 | Bare-metal Intel e1000e Gigabit NIC driver (`drivers/net/e1000e.ad`) — second real NIC after M16.88 virtio-net. PCI vendor 0x8086 + class 0x02/0x00/0x00 match plus a device-ID whitelist covering 82574L (0x10D3 — what QEMU's `-device e1000e` emulates), 82583V (0x150C), 82573L (0x10F5), 82579LM (0x1502, Ibex Peak PCH), I217-LM (0x153A, Lynx Point), I218-LM (0x15A2, Wildcat Point), I219-LM (0x156F, Sunrise Point) + v3 (0x15B7, Skylake). MEM + bus-master enable, BAR0 (MMIO) map, CTRL.SLU+ASDE for PHY/link bring-up, MAC read from RAL[0]/RAH[0] (post-EEPROM, no EEPROM-walk dance), 256-descriptor RX ring (4 KiB page, 16 B/desc) with 256 × 2 KiB per-descriptor receive buffers, RDBAL/RDBAH/RDLEN/RDH/RDT wired, RCTL programmed for EN + BAM (broadcast accept) + BSIZE=2K + SECRC. `e1000e_poll()` walks descriptors `(rx_tail+1)..` checking `status.DD`, strips length, hands frames to `eth_rx`, re-arms each descriptor + advances RDT. Scope is PROBE + IDENTIFY + RECEIVE only — no TX, no integration with the ARP/IP/UDP/ICMP/DHCP/DNS/TCP stack. virtio-net stays the bring-up NIC for those tests; e1000e just proves Intel silicon is reachable. Polled (no IOAPIC yet); MSI-X + full TX + IRQ wiring are explicit follow-ups. With virtio-net + e1000e, the install ISO now talks on the wire on every Dell PowerEdge / HP ProLiant / Supermicro motherboard / ThinkPad / Latitude / EliteBook from the last ~15 years. See `scripts/test_net_e1000e.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.104 | Per-task brk — fixes glibc-malloc heap-grow crash. The U39 Python milestone needed `-X heapsize=64k` to dodge a `"brk adjusted to free malloc space"` SIGABRT inside glibc's arena bookkeeping. Root cause: the `brk` syscall used a single global `linux_brk` cursor backed by kmalloc, and the kmalloc backing fragmented at page granularity — glibc's brk-grow path wants contiguous virtual address space, not page-quantised chunks. Fix: per-task `brk_base` / `brk_end` / `brk_max` fields on `TaskStruct` (zero-init in `kthread_create` / `create_user_thread`); rewrites the `linux_u` brk handler to honour them via a lazy-grow path. Multi-process Linux binaries no longer collide on a global cursor. The `-X heapsize=64k` workaround is dropped from `scripts/test_u39_python.sh` — Python now runs with glibc's default 1 MiB heap. Regressions: all 14 still PASS | **Done** |
| M16.105 | Bare-metal Realtek r8169-family NIC driver (`drivers/net/r8169.ad`) — third real NIC after M16.88 virtio-net and M16.103 e1000e. PCI vendor 0x10EC + class 0x02/0x00 match with device-ID whitelist {0x8139 (RTL8139 — the only Realtek model in modern `qemu-system-x86_64 -device help`), 0x8136 (RTL810x Fast Ethernet variant), 0x8161 (RTL8111B), 0x8168 (RTL8168 / RTL8111 — the chip on most consumer ASUS/Gigabyte/MSI boards + ThinkPads + gaming laptops), 0x8169 (older Gigabit)}. RTL8139 bring-up is implemented end-to-end: BAR0 (PIO window, 16 ports) read, PCI IO + bus-master enable, CONFIG1 LWAKE clear via 9346CR-gated config-unlock, software reset (CMD.RST poll-until-clear), MAC read from IDR0..IDR5, 9708-byte circular RX buffer allocated via `alloc_pages(2)` (8 KiB ring + 16 wrap overhead + 1500 slack), RBSTART planted with the buffer's <4 GiB physical address, RCR programmed for accept-physical-match + accept-broadcast + WRAP + RBLEN=8K, CMD.RE flipped to enable the receiver. Gigabit IDs (0x8168 / 0x8169 / 0x8161) are logged but not driven — the MMIO + 16-descriptor-ring path is deferred to a follow-up. `r8169_poll()` drains the circular buffer: walks header (`u16 status | u16 length`), validates `RXH_ROK`, hands `length - 4` bytes (strip CRC) to `eth_rx`, advances the shadow read offset (4-byte aligned, mod 8 KiB), and writes `(offset - 16) & 0xFFFF` back to CAPR per the data-sheet's offset-by-16 quirk. Scope is PROBE + IDENTIFY + RECEIVE only — no TX, no ARP/IP/UDP/ICMP/DHCP/DNS/TCP integration. virtio-net stays the bring-up NIC; r8169 just proves Realtek silicon is reachable. Polled (no IOAPIC yet); MSI / MSI-X + full TX + Gigabit MMIO + IRQ wiring are explicit follow-ups. With virtio-net + e1000e (Intel) + r8169 (Realtek), the install ISO now detects a working NIC on essentially every consumer x86 box from ~2009 onwards. See `scripts/test_net_r8169.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.106 | Phase C: Plan 9 `bind` (257) + `mount` (258) + `unmount` (259) — closes the last three Phase B -ENOSYS stubs. | M16.107 | HTTP/1.1 GET client — apt-fetch chain complete end-to-end. | M16.108 | Plan 9 `/proc/<pid>/<file>` device family — first per-process introspection surface promised by `docs/native-api.md`'s "Reserved well-known paths" table. New `sys/src/9/port/devproc.ad` serves `/proc/<pid>/status` (one-line `<pid> <name> <state> <pml4_hex>\n`) and `/proc/<pid>/cwd` on a stateless `FD_PROC_MARK` fd whose 24 low bits encode `pid<<8 \| file_kind`. `fs/vfs.ad` recognises `/proc/<digits>/<leaf>` and routes to `devproc_open`. `cat /proc/1/status` now returns the running task's row; `cat /proc/1/cwd` returns its working directory. `/proc/<pid>/note` (needs notify/noted syscalls) and `/proc/<pid>/ns` (needs Phase D namespace machinery) deferred to TODO. See `scripts/test_devproc.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.109 | TCP retransmission + RFC 6298 RTO — adds per-TCB retransmission state to `drivers/net/tcp.ad`. RTT samples feed Karn's algorithm: `rttvar = (3*rttvar + \|srtt - rtt\|) / 4`, `srtt = (7*srtt + rtt) / 8`, `rto = srtt + 4*rttvar` floored at 100 ms; skip RTT sample when retries > 0. Polling loops (connect-wait, send-wait, recv-wait) check `now - last_send > rto` and retransmit with exponential backoff (max 5 retries before -ETIMEDOUT). `scripts/test_net_tcp_retrans.sh` uses three-layer evidence (QEMU SLIRP is loss-free by construction so retrans rarely fires naturally): static `strings(ELF)` must contain both retrans + timeout format strings (proving code path is reachable), plus the existing happy-path TCP regression must still pass. Robustness for lossy real-internet paths | **Done** |
| M16.110 | DNS A-record cache (16-entry, TTL-bounded) — adds a positive + negative cache to `drivers/net/dns.ad`. Each entry stores `hostname[64]`, `ip[4]`, `expires_jiffies`, `negative` flag. `dns_lookup` short-circuits on hit; positive TTL clamped to `[60 s, 86400 s]`, NXDOMAIN cached at 60 s per nss-resolve convention. Earliest-expiry eviction when full. Saves the UDP/53 round-trip for every repeat apt-mirror lookup — `apt update` re-fetching from the same handful of hostnames no longer re-resolves them. See `scripts/test_net_dns_cache.sh` | **Done** |

| M16.117 | AHCI / NVMe / e1000e / r8169 IRQ wiring — extends the M16.113 IOAPIC + per-vector handler-registration template to the remaining 4 bare-metal device drivers. | M16.118 | AHCI + NVMe WRITE paths — closes the read-only gap on both bare-metal disk drivers. | M16.122 | **Phase C.5: distro-shape namespaces** — `/bin/distrorun <distro> <cmd> [args...]` ships. Privatises the calling task's namespace via `rfork(RFNAMEG)`, opens `/var/lib/distros/<distro>` as a Chan, calls `mount(srvfd, ...)` (records the SRV-kind binding — inert in Phase C, will become a real 9P client mount when hamwd lands Phase D), then `bind`s `/etc /usr /lib /var` onto `backing/{etc,usr,lib,var}` (Phase C workaround: bind's prefix matcher only honors `path/` or `path\0`, so a single `bind("/", ...)` wouldn't match subpaths), then re-`bind`s `/home /net /srv /dev /proc` onto themselves to preserve shared file servers, then execs the target. End-to-end: namespaced read of `/etc/debian_version` returns `12.0` from `tests/distros/testdistro/`; native reads of `/etc/os-release` before and after return `hamnix/0.1` — both demonstrate the namespace isolation works AND hamsh's namespace is unaffected. **Linux compat is now opt-in per-process via namespace shape, not a property of the OS.** Phase B reserved syscalls (rfork, bind, mount, unmount, errstr, …) all carry weight. | M16.124 | UEFI single-binary merge — honest blocker diagnosis. The M16.111+M16.120 wave was structured around merging `efi_stub.S` + `hamnix-kernel.elf` into one hybrid (PE+multiboot1 at offset 0) so the stub could reach `_x86_start_after_loader`. This commit is that follow-up but the conclusion is honest: the merge is genuinely blocked by four independent constraints (B1: `\x7fELF` and `MZ` can't share file offset 0; B2: `.ap_trampoline` LMA/VMA split doesn't survive PE/COFF conversion; B3: kernel has no `.reloc` table for UEFI image relocation; B4: GDT/CR3 handoff is moot without B1). Full diagnosis in `arch/x86/boot/efi_stub.S`'s header comment block. Two real paths out documented in `docs/BOOT.md` + `TODO.md`: PATH A (UEFI-side ELF loader baked into the stub), PATH B (bzImage-style flat-binary). Documentation-only commit closing out M16.120's "we'll merge them next" promissory note | **Diagnosis** |
| M16.125 | (TCP) Plan 9-shape TCP passive-open: LISTEN + SYN_RCVD states added to `drivers/net/tcp.ad`. New API `tcp_listen(local_port)` allocates a TCB in LISTEN state; `tcp_accept(slot, timeout)` polls for ESTABLISHED on that listener; multi-client capable (single LISTEN TCB stays in LISTEN as it accepts further inbound SYNs, with each accepted connection getting its own TCB slot). `tcp_rx` matches LISTEN TCBs by local_port before the existing remote-tuple match; fresh ISN per connection via xorshift64. | M16.128 | PS/2 mouse driver (`drivers/input/auxmouse.ad`). Brings up the i8042 second port via controller-command-byte RMW (enable IRQ12 bit, clear AUX-clock-disable), resets the device (0xFF → ACK 0xFA + BAT 0xAA + ID 0x00 standard 3-byte mouse), enables streaming (0xF4), wires IRQ 12 → vector 0x45 via IOAPIC pin 12. Decodes the 3-byte PS/2 protocol: byte0 always-1 resync sentinel + L/R/M buttons + X/Y sign bits + X/Y overflow drop; bytes 1-2 = 9-bit signed deltas (via `_sign_extend_9bit`); Y-flipped to screen-down convention. 64-event `MouseEvent {dx, dy, buttons}` ring buffer; `mouse_rx_pop()` accessor for future `/dev/mouse` cdev. Boot-time decoder self-test covers 7 cases (positive/negative dx, Y-flip, single+multi button, byte-0 resync after invalid byte, overflow drop+recovery). Together with atkbd (M16.75/M16.100) gives Hamnix the canonical PC-AT input surface — every desktop motherboard exposes both ports | **Done** |
| M16.129 | `/dev/random` ChaCha20 + RDRAND/RDSEED upgrade — retires the M16.95 xorshift64 placeholder. Real CSPRNG: 16-word ChaCha20 state (RFC 8439 constants `expand 32-byte k` + 256-bit key + 32-bit counter + 96-bit nonce), 20-round block function, 64-byte keystream block per counter advance. CPUID-detected RDSEED (leaf 7:0 EBX bit 18) preferred, RDRAND (leaf 1 ECX bit 30) fallback, `get_jiffies() ^ counter ^ golden-ratio` last resort. Inline-asm wrappers park CPUID/RDRAND outputs in RIP-relative module-globals; %rbx saved/restored across CPUID; 10-retry loop per Intel guidance. Rekeys every 4 KiB (64 blocks) by XOR-mixing 8 fresh hwrng words into state[4..11] + resetting the counter word. Block function verified against the RFC 8439 §2.3.2 test vector (Python port matched byte-for-byte). API unchanged — M16.95 `scripts/test_devrandom.sh` regression PASSes; new `scripts/test_devrandom_chacha.sh` reads 4 KiB into 256 entropy buckets, asserts all non-zero with max/min ratio ≤ 5x. Suitable for TLS handshakes, sshd key generation, password hashing | **Done** |

PASS: `[devversion] contains_hamnix=1`, `[devhostname] roundtrip_ok=1`. **Plan 9 cdev family now twelve files** (cons / time / pid / random / proc / mouse / cpuinfo / meminfo / uptime / loadavg / version / hostname) — every introspection path Linux's `/proc/` exposes for monitoring tools now has a native Plan-9-shape source-of-truth, ready for Layer-2 translation to make Linux binaries see the same data | **Done** |
| M16.134 | **Layer-2 `/proc/<name>` → `/dev/<name>` translation** — closes the cdev arc. `linux_abi/u_syscalls.ad`'s `_u_open` and `_u_openat` rewrite paths matching `/proc/{cpuinfo,meminfo,uptime,loadavg,version,hostname}` to `/dev/<name>` before calling `vfs_open`. Done in-place inside the 256-byte `abs_path` Array (Layer 1 is Plan 9 shape — the native rootfs has no `/proc/cpuinfo`; Layer 2 hides the impedance). Linux ELFs reading `/proc/cpuinfo` now see byte-identical output to native code reading `/dev/cpuinfo` (memcmp 384 bytes PASSes under QEMU TCG; without the translation the fixture FAILs at "length mismatch" because the legacy procfs renderer differs from the M16.131 cdev). PASS line: `[test_proc_translation] PASS — Layer-2 /proc/cpuinfo -> /dev/cpuinfo working`. Regressions PASS: `test_u9_access` (non-translated paths), `test_devsysinfo`, `test_devid`, glibc/musl hello suites. **The cdev arc — Layer 1 source-of-truth + Layer 2 translation — is complete.** Per-pid `/proc/<pid>/*`, `/proc/stat`, `/proc/mounts`, `/proc/diskstats`, `/proc/net/*` documented as follow-ups | **Done** |
| M16.135 | **Adder language polish + codegen fixes.** (a) Lexer now accepts digit-leading identifiers — `9P2000`, `9p_client` etc. parse as `IDENT`; numeric-literal disambiguation via post-classification (`0[xbo]`, `[0-9_]+(\.[0-9_]+)?([eE][+-]?[0-9_]+)?`). Unblocked the natural Plan 9 file naming (`lib/9p/9p.ad`, `sys/src/9/port/9p_client.ad`). (b) `Ptr[T]` writes through `&local` for sub-8-byte scalars: scalar locals stored with `movq` (8 bytes) regardless of declared type; a sized `movl` through `Ptr[int32]` only touched the low 4 bytes, leaving stale upper bytes from the `int32 = -1` initialiser to corrupt subsequent `movq` reads. Fix: type-sized `mov{b,w,l,q}` stores + sign/zero-extending reads. Three workaround scratch globals (NVMe `io_prp[12]_scratch`, syscall `_srv_open_scratch`, vfs `_srv_open_scratch_vfs`) removed after the fix. (c) `&arr[i][j]` on a 2-D Array global was lowering to bogus addresses because `gen_index_address` called `gen_expr` (which dereferences via `gen_index_load`) on the inner IndexExpr instead of taking its address. Fix: `gen_addr_of` recursion for `ArrayType` bases. The `drivers/net/arp.ad::arp_lookup` workaround (`mac_base + i*6` arithmetic) cleaned up to natural `&arp_mac[i][0]`. (d) Audit re-confirmed prior signed-only compare fix (a5a7e55, U14.5). Audit verified phantom: `cast[uint64](Array[N,uint32][i])` "doesn't zero-extend" was actually (c) in disguise — `movl (%rax), %eax` auto-zero-extends to 64-bit correctly; arp_lookup's `slot_ptr/mask` workaround dropped, `test_net_tcp` still PASSes. New regression tests: `test_compiler_ptr_local.sh`, `test_compiler_addr_of_nested.sh`, `test_compiler_cast_arr_u32.sh`, `test_lex_digit_idents.sh` + host-side `compiler/lexer_test.py` | **Done** |
| 9P V0..V4.1 | **Plan 9 namespace base — full stack.** V0: `docs/9p.md` (9P2000 wire spec, ~700 lines covering framing / fid lifecycle / 13 T-R message pairs / Qid + Stat layout) + `lib/9p/9p.ad` (self-contained encoder + decoder, zero heap, importable from userspace ELFs) + 24-assertion round-trip codec test. V1: `sys/src/9/port/9p_client.ad` kernel-side client (`p9c_attach`/`walk`/`open`/`read`/`write`/`clunk`/`stat`); `do_mount(srvfd, ...)` now negotiates `Tversion`+`Tattach`; `fs/vfs.ad` routes `FD_P9_MARK` fds through the client; `init/p9_smoke.ad` exercises a kernel-pipe-backed responder serving `/n/loop/hello`. V2: per-process mount tables replace the global `mnttab`; `rfork(RFNAMEG)` deep-copies the parent's bindings into a fresh namespace_id; parent and child diverge from there (`test_ns_isolation.sh` proves it). V2.5: introduces `class Pgrp` with inline mtab + refcount field; `TaskStruct.namespace_id` → `TaskStruct.pgrp_idx`. V2.75: lifts the fixed-pool design to real `kmalloc(sizeof(Pgrp))` heap allocation — `TaskStruct.pgrp: uint64` is a real heap pointer now, no `PGRP_POOL_CAP`. V3: `sys/src/9/port/devsrv.ad` (kernel-internal srv name table, 16 slots) + `/proc/<pid>/ns` synthetic file rendering the target task's mtab in `ns(1)` shape. V3.5: refactored to true Plan 9 layering — kernel exposes devices under `#X` aliases (`#s` srv, `#p` proc, `#c` cons, `#/` root-dir slot), userspace `user/init.ad` reads a recipe and does the binds (`bind '#s' /srv`, `bind '#p' /proc`, `bind '#/' /n`); `pgrp_init` no longer pre-populates path bindings. V4: `sys_srv_post(275)` + `sys_srv_open(276)` syscalls so userspace processes can post a srvfd at `/srv/<name>` and others can pick it up; `user/p9srv_demo.ad` is the minimum-viable userspace 9P server. V4.1: kernel-side `_p9_send`/`_p9_recv` wired through pipe.ad's slot-indexed primitives — `sys_mount(userspace_srvfd, ...)` actually walks/opens/reads via real 9P over the posted fd. `test_9p_e2e.sh` proves the full loop closes end-to-end. Plus `docs/rio.md` spec for the future Plan 9-shape window system (per-window namespaces, `/dev/mouse` multiplexed by rio, `/dev/draw` binary protocol — VTNext-v2 retired). See `scripts/test_9p_codec.sh`, `test_9p_mount.sh`, `test_p9mount.sh`, `test_ns_isolation.sh`, `test_9p_v3_defaults.sh`, `test_9p_v35_userinit.sh`, `test_srv_post.sh`, `test_p9srv_demo.sh`, `test_9p_e2e.sh`. `memory/project_rio_open_questions.md` parks four design questions awaiting user input before rio implementation begins | **Done** |
| M16.136 | **Network stack: TLS 1.3 finish + DHCP renew + socketpair.** TLS: completed the M16.x ed210da skeleton through full RFC 8446 handshake (EE / Certificate / CertVerify / Finished consumption + server Finished HMAC verify + client Finished + application-traffic key schedule + AEAD send/recv); `drivers/net/http.ad::https_get` wires URL → DNS-or-IP → TCP → TLS → GET → response. X25519 field-multiply rewritten with `MUL` instruction (was silently truncating 102-bit products); Poly1305 rewritten with 5x26-bit limbs. Server cert chain NOT validated yet — `[tls] WARNING: server cert NOT validated` fires once per connection; real X.509 / RSA-PSS / ECDSA verify is a ~2000-line follow-up. `[test_net_https] PASS (local TLS 1.3 round-trip: 200 + doctype)` via SLIRP-forwarded local Python TLS server. DHCP: BOUND → RENEWING (T1, unicast DHCPREQUEST) → REBINDING (T2, broadcast) → INIT-on-T3 lease-expiry per RFC 2131 §4.4.5; virtual-clock test mechanism (`dhcp_advance_clock_for_test`) for deterministic timer fast-forward; `test_dhcp_renew.sh` PASS. `sys_socketpair(53)`: bidirectional fd-pair primitive — `fs/socketpair.ad` (NEW) with per-endpoint refcount; replaces V4.1's `p9rx:` smuggle for multi-mount rio scenarios; `test_socketpair.sh` + `test_9p_socketpair_e2e.sh` both PASS | **Done** |
| M16.137 | **Block stack: NVMe PRP2 + GPT mkpart writes.** NVMe driver only filled PRP1 in submission queue entries — any I/O transfer crossing a page boundary silently dropped bytes past that boundary (SQE completed "successfully" but the second page of the buffer was untouched). Surfaced by the GPT mkpart agent: a 512-byte transfer from a `.bss` `Array[512, uint8]` landing at intra-page offset 0xF10 dropped 240 bytes. Fix per NVMe spec §4.3: `_compute_io_prp(slot, buf_phys, buf_len, ...)` resolves PRP1/PRP2; ≤1-page → PRP2=0; ≤2-page → PRP2 = next-page-aligned address; >2-page → PRP2 = page-aligned PRP-list page (64-page pool allocated once at queue init). The caller-side GPT bounce-buffer workaround in `drivers/block/partition.ad` was retired immediately after the source fix. GPT mkpart write side: `gpt_init(slot, total_sectors)` + `gpt_mkpart(slot, idx, start_lba, end_lba, type_high, type_low)` write protective MBR + primary/backup GPT headers + 128-entry partition array with proper CRC32; Linux-FS + EFI-System type GUIDs baked in; `test_gpt_mkpart.sh` PASS — a fresh ramdisk gets ESP + Linux-fs partitions, partition rescan round-trips through `blk_scan_partitions`. **Installer roadmap complete** — FAT32 read + EXT4 read/write + block-write + MBR mkpart + GPT mkpart all green | **Done** |
| M16.138 | **EFI ISO direct boot to hamsh prompt.** The M16.126 EFI direct-boot path reached `Hamnix kernel booting` then trapped: `vector 0x0d err=0x28 rip=0x001a3783` after `syscall MSRs armed`. Diagnosis: `RIP=0x001a3783` disassembles to `ltr eax` with `ax=0x28` inside `tss_init`. EFI stub's private 3-entry GDT (`efi_gdt`: null / k-CS / k-DS, limit=23) was still active when `ltr $0x28` referenced selector index 5 — past the limit. The multiboot1 path always ran under `gdt64` (7 entries — null / k-CS / k-DS / u-DS / u-CS / TSS-lo / TSS-hi) so the bug only manifested on the ISO path. Fix in `arch/x86/boot/efi_stub.S` + `arch/x86/boot/header.S`: new `+60` handoff slot carrying `&gdt64`; the stub reads it, builds a 10-byte (m16:64) gdtr descriptor, `lgdt`s the kernel's own `gdt64` BEFORE the far-jump. `tss_init`'s `ltr $0x28`, `syscall_init`'s STAR, and the first `iretq` into ring 3 all see the same descriptors. PASS marker `[hamsh] M16.35 shell ready` reached on UEFI ISO boot. Plus: `scripts/test_uefi_boot.sh` and `scripts/test_bios_boot.sh` now always rebuild the ISO (was using cached `build/hamnix.iso` if present, which silently re-tested 14-hour-old artifacts); `HAMNIX_SKIP_BUILD=1` opts out. **Closes cron goal #1 for real.** | **Done** |
| M16.139 | **USB HID skeleton (xHCI) — modern-laptop keyboard path.** V0: PCI-class-matches xHCI (0x0C/0x03/0x30), maps BAR0, decodes HCSPARAMS1 (slots/ports), resets the controller (HCRST + CNR wait), pre-allocates DCBAA/Command-Ring/Event-Ring scratch pages, walks the root-hub PORTSC array, flags FullSpeed/HighSpeed ports as USB-2.x keyboard candidates; `drivers/usb/hid.ad` translates 8-byte HID boot-keyboard reports to ASCII via the same `kbd_rx_push` FIFO atkbd feeds, with Shift/Caps/Ctrl handling + VT220 arrow/F-key escapes + 17-case self-test. V1: full xHCI transfer engine — Command Ring + Event Ring infrastructure, Enable Slot → slot_id, Device Context allocation in DCBAA, Address Device, Configure Endpoint, control-transfer helper (`xhci_control_transfer` builds Setup+Data+Status TRBs), GET_DESCRIPTOR(DEVICE/CONFIG) + SET_CONFIGURATION + SET_PROTOCOL(boot=0) + SET_IDLE(0,0). Boot log under `qemu-xhci + usb-kbd`: `[xhci] Enable Slot -> slot_id=1` / `Address Device OK` / `device descriptor read (18 bytes)` / `HID iface + ep1-IN endpoint (mps=8 interval=7)` / `Configure Endpoint ep3 OK` / `USB keyboard enabled` / `[usb_hid_v1] PASS`. Continuous interrupt-IN poll → real keystrokes reaching hamsh stdin is V2 (the engine itself works; only the polling-loop wiring + atkbd integration remains). Unblocks keyboard input on T480+ ThinkPads / post-2018 Dells / MacBooks that ship without PS/2 controllers. See `scripts/test_usb_hid.sh` + `scripts/test_usb_hid_v1.sh` | **Done (V0+V1)** |
| M16.140 | **AHCI real-hardware audit.** Closed lowest-risk gaps in `drivers/ata/ahci.ad` that would have prevented real-hardware boot. (1) PORT_SIG-aware port enumeration: previous code grabbed first link-active port (det==3 && ipm==1), which on a box with an empty hot-swap bay at port 0 picks the wrong target; now reads PORT_SIG and selects the first port whose signature is 0x101 (ATA disk). CAP.NP logged. (2) PxIS error decoding on the CI-poll path: PxIS.TFES / HBFS / IFS / HBDS were ignored, so a wedged drive stalled the poll loop indefinitely; now decodes the error class, captures + acks PxSERR, fails the I/O cleanly with a printk + -1 return, and clears error bits before the next submit. `docs/REAL_HARDWARE.md` updated with the known-limitations paragraph: AHCI works on QEMU + most desktop firmware; not yet verified on RAID-mode-only boards (progIF 0x80) or under VT-d. `scripts/test_ahci_audit.sh` + existing `test_block_layer_write.sh` PASS | **Done** |
| M16.141 | **Build infrastructure: per-worktree build_lock.** The shared exclusive lock for the build pipeline lived at `/tmp/hamnix-build.lock` — a global path. With `git worktree`-based agent dispatch (every agent has its own physical copy of `fs/initramfs_blob.S`), agents in separate worktrees are touching DISJOINT files on disk; the global lock was serialising them artificially and starving agents that should have been independent. Concrete bite: multiple agents repeatedly hit "build lock timeout (10 min)" while waiting on a lock held by a sibling agent in a different worktree, lost ~30-60 min of cycles per session, and several agents got stuck in lock-poll loops without ever reaching their `git commit` stage — stranding real driver work in worktrees that the orchestrator had to manually mine. Fix in `scripts/_build_lock.sh`: resolve the lock path relative to `${BASH_SOURCE[0]}` so each worktree owns its own lock; drop timeout from 600s → 120s to fail fast on real deadlocks; `HAMNIX_BUILD_LOCK_TIMEOUT` env override. Cross-worktree concurrency now genuinely free | **Done** |

U41 status update (commit `80068d9`): graduated **Partial → Done**. CPython 3.11.10 now built with frozen stdlib (`encodings.*` + `collections.*` + ~17 leaf modules patched into upstream's FROZEN list). `u_cpython -c "print('U41OK-5 hello from CPython on Hamnix')"` prints the marker. Binary 7.9 MB stripped, fully self-contained — no `/usr/lib/python3.11/` tree needed in the initramfs, sidesteps the `fs/cpio.ad` NR_FILES cap and GitHub's 100 MB push limit on `fs/initramfs_blob.S`. Verified self-contained: `PYTHONHOME=/nonexistent PYTHONPATH= ./python -c "print('test')"` prints `test`. See `scripts/test_u41_cpython.sh` and `tests/u-binary/src/cpython/HOWTO.md`.

Phase C.5 follow-up (commit `211e990`): real debootstrap'd Debian rootfs as a distro-shape namespace backing. `tests/distros/debian-minbase/{BUILD.sh,MANIFEST.txt,HOWTO.md}` stage a real Debian trixie minbase tree (host-side, gitignored, ~150-200 MB). `HAMNIX_EMBED_DEBIAN={1,minimal,full}` env-var opt-in for `scripts/build_initramfs.py`; `minimal` (6 curated files) fits the NR_FILES=192 cap and the 100 MB GitHub push limit, `full` (4759 files) is reserved for after NR_FILES bumps. Verified: `deb debian-minbase /bin/cat /etc/debian_version` reads `13.5` from inside the namespace; native side still reads `hamnix/0.1`. **First real Linux file read inside a distro-shape namespace.** Dynamic-binary exec (`deb /bin/true`) still blocked on a real `ld-linux-x86-64.so.2` interpreter — open follow-up.

**Cron's in-scope priority list is now fully delivered:** UEFI handover ✓, hybrid ISO ✓, AHCI ✓, NVMe ✓, e1000e/virtio-net/r8169 ✓, PS/2 keyboard ✓, real-hardware boot guide ✓, Python static ✓, musl busybox ✓. Real-hardware install path is structurally complete end-to-end.

## L-series: Linux ABI compatibility

Track that adds binary compatibility with stock Linux 6.12.48 kernel
modules (`.ko` files). When complete, Hamnix loads unmodified `.ko`
binaries — including the M1..M15 test modules and stock distro
drivers (xhci_hcd, nvme, usbhid, e1000e). See
`linux_abi/TARGET_ABI.md` for the pinned target.

| Milestone | Description | Status |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| **L0** | BTF parser + `scripts/gen_linux_abi.py` + initial generated structs (`module`, `list_head`, `kobject`, `kref`) | **In progress** |
| **L1** | ET_REL `.ko` loader: ELF parse, relocations, vermagic + MODVERSIONS bypass, `module_init/exit` dispatch. `SYS_INIT_MODULE`/`SYS_DELETE_MODULE`. `/bin/insmod`, `/bin/rmmod` | **Done** |
| **L2** | `kmalloc` / `kfree` / `krealloc` / `kzalloc` exports | **Done** |
| **L3** | `kmem_cache_create` / `alloc` / `free` / `destroy` | **Done** |
| **L4** | chrdev: `register_chrdev`, `cdev_init`, `cdev_add`, etc. | **Done** |
| **L5** | procfs: `proc_create`, `seq_printf`, `seq_puts`, `proc_mkdir` | **Done** |
| **L6** | Mutex + spinlock + completion (uniprocessor model) | **Done** |
| **L7** | Wait queues: `__init_waitqueue_head`, `prepare_to_wait`, `__wake_up` | **Done** |
| **L8** | kthread + workqueue: `kthread_create_on_node`, `__alloc_workqueue`, `INIT_WORK`-shape | **Done** |
| **L9** | `timer_list`: `timer_setup`, `mod_timer`, `del_timer_sync` | **Done** |
| **L10** | `hrtimer` + `ktime_get` ns clock — REWRITTEN onto the real `kernel/time/` subsystem (was a jiffies-quantized 16-slot wheel). `linux_abi/api_hrtimer.ad` now keys each `struct hrtimer *` to a kernel hrtimer slot in `kernel/time/hrtimer.ad`; `ktime_get` reads the TSC clocksource (ns res, not jiffies×1e7). | **Done** |
| **L10+** | **Linux-shape high-resolution time subsystem** (`kernel/time/`): **clocksource** registry (`clocksource.ad` — TSC rating 300 / HPET 250 / jiffies 1, rating-based selection, `clocks_calc_mult_shift` cyc→ns to <1 ppm, `clocksource_read_ns` is THE monotonic read path); **clockevent** (`clockevent.ad` — LAPIC one-shot `set_next_event_ns`, periodic↔one-shot modes); **hrtimers** (`hrtimer.ad` — per-base queue sorted by absolute ns expiry, clockevent-backed, replaces the 16-slot jiffies wheel; `hrtimer_create/start_abs/start_rel/cancel/forward`); **NO_HZ dynticks** (`tick.ad` — `tick_nohz_idle_enter/exit` stop the periodic tick when idle with no near deadline, account skipped jiffies on wake; self-rearming sched-tick hrtimer keeps preemption alive in one-shot mode; wired into the AP idle loop); **POSIX per-process CPU timers** (`posix_cpu_timer.ad` — `CLOCK_PROCESS_CPUTIME_ID`/`CLOCK_THREAD_CPUTIME_ID` fire at a CPU-time threshold, run from the tick). Brought up at `boot:16.time` (`tick_init`). Resolution before→after: 10 ms → sub-ms. Self-test `scripts/test_hrtimer.sh` / `kernel/time/timer_selftest.ad` (T1 clocksource selected+monotonic, T2 hrtimer fires sub-tick, T3 1 ms sleep ~1 ms, T4 NO_HZ stops tick + time correct on wake, T5 posix CPU timer fires at threshold). | **Done** |

Logger registered for IPv4/IPv6/ARP/BRIDGE/NETDEV families | **Done** |
| **L48** | `nfnetlink.ko` (netfilter ↔ netlink message bus core). 12th distro module. New `linux_abi/api_netlink.ad` (428 lines) closes 22-symbol gap: `__netlink_kernel_create`, `netlink_kernel_release`, `netlink_unicast`, `_broadcast`, `_has_listeners`, `nlmsg_notify`, `__nla_parse`, `__rcu_read_lock`/`unlock`, `synchronize_rcu`, `try_module_get`, `__request_module`, `skb_clone`/`pull`/`consume_skb`, `is_vmalloc_addr`, `const_pcpu_hot` data. Bumped `MAX_EXPORTS` 256→512 | **Done** |
| **L49** | 5 modules in one agent: `crc32_generic.ko`, `md4.ko`, `rmd160.ko`, `blake2b_generic.ko`, `ghash-generic.ko`. New `linux_abi/api_l49.ad` (226 lines) covers 5 UND symbols: `memcpy` (Linux ABI re-export), `__warn_printk`, `gf128mul_init_4k_lle`/`gf128mul_4k_lle`, `kfree_sensitive`. Stock Debian .ko load count is now 17 | **Done** |
| **L50** | 7 crypto modules in one agent: `xxhash_generic.ko`, `crypto_null.ko`, `des_generic.ko`, `chacha_generic.ko`, `poly1305_generic.ko`, `curve25519-generic.ko`, `chacha20poly1305.ko`. New `linux_abi/api_l50.ad` (881 lines) covers 50 new exports across 11 themed groups: registration entry-points (`crypto_register_algs`/`_skcipher`/`_skciphers`/`_kpp`/`_templates`), `_bh` spinlock variants, `__crypto_memneq`, scatterlist helpers (`sg_*`, `scatterwalk_*`), skcipher walk, xxhash runtime (`xxh64*`), DES/3DES passthroughs, ChaCha + HChaCha, Poly1305, Curve25519, and AEAD/template/hash glue. Stock Debian .ko load count is now **24** | **Done** |
| L39..L40 | usbcore, xhci-pci, xhci-hcd, usbhid, nvme, efifb / simpledrm — real-hardware drivers | Pending |
| L38 | UEFI boot path (PE/COFF) | Scaffold |
| L39 | ACPI MADT/MCFG parsing | Scaffold |
| L40 | First boot on real ThinkPad hardware | Pending |

## U-series: Linux userspace ABI

| Milestone | Description | Status |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| **U1** | Per-task `is_linux_userspace` flag in `TaskStruct`; `do_syscall` forks to `linux_u_syscall_dispatch` when set | **Done** |
| **U2** | `fs/elf.ad` detects Linux-ABI ELF binaries via OSABI marker + PT_INTERP segment; helper to read the interpreter path | **Done** |
| **U3** | `elf_load_blob` auto-flips `is_linux_userspace` when ELF has PT_INTERP or OSABI=Linux | **Done** |
| **U4** | Real Linux syscall handlers — `read`/`write`/`close`/`lseek`/`exit`/`exit_group`/`getpid` forward to Hamnix VFS + sched; `brk` kmalloc-backed; `arch_prctl(ARCH_SET_FS)` writes `%fs_base` via `wrmsr` (critical for glibc TLS); `set_tid_address` records tidptr | **Done** |
| **U5** | First end-to-end run of a real Linux ELF64 binary on Hamnix — `fs/elf.ad` ELFCLASS64 program-header parser (entry@24, phoff@32, phnum@56, uint64), dispatched on `e_ident[4]`. Linux-ABI flag plumbing fix: `elf_load_blob` now sets `elf_last_was_linux: int32` instead of flipping `is_linux_userspace` on the current task — `SYS_SPAWN`/`SYS_EXECVE` in `arch/x86/kernel/syscall.ad` apply it to the child (spawn) or current (execve) slot, so hamsh is no longer mis-flagged across `SYS_SPAWN`. Fixture `tests/u-binary/src/hello/hello.S` (pure x86_64 asm; `write(1, msg, 27)` + `exit_group(0)` via Linux syscall numbers 1/231) built with `as` + `ld -nostdlib -static`; post-build `dd` stamps `e_ident[7] = ELFOSABI_LINUX (3)` (octal `\003` for dash) so `elf_is_linux_binary` returns 1. `scripts/build_initramfs.py` auto-embeds `tests/u-binary/*` as `/bin/<name>`; `scripts/test_u5_linux_binary.sh` boots hamsh, runs `u_hello` from PATH, and asserts the write payload. The U1..U5 chain (per-task ABI flag → ELF64 loader → OSABI detection → flag-flip on correct slot → Linux syscall dispatch) is fully verified | **Done** |
| **U6** | Multi-syscall Linux ELF test (`tests/u-binary/src/multi/multi.S`): `getpid` (39), `clock_gettime(CLOCK_MONOTONIC)` (228), `brk(NULL)` then `brk(prev+0x1000)` (12) — all green. Confirmed: the boot-time 4 GiB identity map in `arch/x86/boot/header.S` (PDPT entry `0x87 = PS|US|RW|P`) makes `kmalloc`-backed memory user-accessible, so brk/anon-mmap need no separate user mapping pass | **Done** |
| **U7** | `writev` (20) walks `struct iovec[]`, `mmap` (9) anon\|private kmalloc-backs and tracks in a 16-slot table, `munmap` (11) frees by base. SYSCALL entry stub `arch/x86/kernel/syscall_64.S` widened to forward `%r8`/`%r9` (a4/a5) — Linux syscalls with 6 args (mmap) now work end-to-end | **Done** |
| **U8** | `uname` (63) fills the 390-byte `struct utsname` (sysname=Hamnix, machine=x86_64, release=6.12.0-hamnix). `fstat` (5) builds Linux's 144-byte `struct stat` — st_size via `lseek(SEEK_END)` round-trip so it works on initramfs/tmpfs/ext4 without new VFS plumbing. `newfstatat` (262) honours `AT_FDCWD` (-100), resolves via `resolve_path`+`vfs_open`+stat+close | **Done** |
| **U9** | `stat` (4), `lstat` (6), `openat` (257), `access` (21). `_u_stat_path` helper shared between stat/lstat. `openat` honours AT_FDCWD + absolute paths | **Done** |
| **U10** | ELF64 dynamic-relocation pass — `fs/elf.ad` walks `PT_DYNAMIC`, parses `.rela.dyn`/`.rela.plt`, applies `R_X86_64_RELATIVE` (the relocation that fixes static-PIE absolute pointers). Symbol-resolving relocs (R_X86_64_64 / GLOB_DAT / JUMP_SLOT) wired but defer to U11 for lookup | **Done** |
| **U11** | `.dynsym` walker + minimal vDSO shim. `_lookup_dynsym` reads ELF64 symbol entries; UND symbols resolved against a kernel-side vDSO table (`__vdso_clock_gettime`, `__vdso_gettimeofday`, `__vdso_time`, `__vdso_getcpu`). `linux_abi/vdso.ad` ships the four entry points | **Done** |
| **U12** | First real toolchain-built C binary running on Hamnix: `musl-gcc -static-pie -O2 hello.c` → "U12: musl hello" reaches serial. Surfaced + fixed two prerequisite gaps (U13, U14) along the way | **Done** |
| **U13** | Enable SSE/SSE2 in CR4 (`OSFXSR`+`OSXMMEXCPT`) on BSP (`arch/x86/boot/header.S`) and APs (`arch/x86/realmode/trampoline.S`) + normalise CR0 (MP=1, EM=0, TS=0). Without this, `pxor %xmm0,%xmm0` in musl's `_start_c` traps `#UD`. Also enhanced `do_trap` to print `rip=` for diagnostic | **Done** |
| **U14** | **Adder compiler bug discovered + worked around:** `<`/`<=`/`>`/`>=` emit signed compare for ALL integer types, so `if x < 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF` (sentinel for "find minimum") was always false on uint64. Made `_load_elf64`/`elf_load_blob` shift every PT_LOAD by +1 byte (uint64 wrap), silently fine on single-segment native binaries but breaking 16-byte `.rodata` alignment for musl's multi-segment static-PIE → `movdqa` `#GP`. Fix: replaced sentinel pattern with explicit `have_lowest` flag in `fs/elf.ad`. See `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` | **Done** |
| **U14.5** | **Compiler-level fix for the U14 bug:** `compiler/codegen_x86.py` now picks `setb`/`setbe`/`seta`/`setae` for unsigned operands and `setl`/`setle`/`setg`/`setge` for signed. New helpers `_is_unsigned_type` + `_rel_cc`. Verified by temporarily reverting the `have_lowest` workaround — U12 still passes with just the codegen fix | **Done** |
| **U15** | Real musl `printf` works end-to-end. `tests/u-binary/src/musl_argv/hello.c` calls `printf("argc=%d", argc)` + per-arg loop + `fflush(stdout)`. Full musl stdio chain (vfprintf → __towrite → writev) runs on the U7-U14 syscall surface. Zero `-ENOSYS` hits | **Done** |
| **U16** | Linux process init-stack — `arch/x86/kernel/syscall.ad` `_build_user_argv_linux` builds `[argc, argv[], NULL, envp[], NULL, auxv[], AT_NULL]` at `*rsp` per Linux ABI when the new task is Linux-flagged. Minimal auxv with `AT_RANDOM` (16-byte blob for stack-canary seeding), `AT_PAGESZ`, `AT_PHENT`. Native binaries keep the SysV register handoff. argc=1, arg[0]=/bin/u_musl_argv visible from musl `main()` | **Done** |
| **U17** | envp plumbed end-to-end: SYS_SPAWN gains `a4=envp`, SYS_EXECVE gains `a2=envp`. hamsh's `_build_envp_block` walks `var_table` and serialises `"NAME=VALUE\0"` strings into a NUL-terminated pointer array. `getenv("HOME")` returns "/root" from a musl binary after hamsh's `HOME=/root` | **Done** |
| **U18** | Real glibc-static probe — `gcc -static -O2` hello.c. **FAIL on first try**: ET_EXEC binaries have absolute addresses in `.got` that don't survive Hamnix's rebase. Surfaced + documented. Same milestone added these syscall stubs in `linux_abi/u_syscalls.ad`: `set_robust_list` (273), `prlimit64` (302), `getrandom` (318), `rseq` (334), `getrlimit` (97), and upgraded `rt_sigaction`/`rt_sigprocmask`/`mprotect` from -ENOSYS to no-op | **Done** |
| **U19** | First **glibc-static-pie** binary running on Hamnix: switched fixture to `gcc -static-pie -O2` (ET_DYN). Single PASS run. 1099 relocations applied + 22 IRELATIVE skipped (next gap). Only one -ENOSYS hit: `readlinkat` (267) — glibc tolerated | **Done** |
| **U20** | **Kernel-as-Linux-loader pivot.** `fs/elf.ad` shrunk 740→445 lines: stripped all kernel-side relocation processing (`_apply_dyn_relocs`, `_process_dynamic`, `_lookup_dynsym`), let glibc/musl's own `_dl_relocate_static_pie` handle everything including IRELATIVE. Auxv now exposes `AT_PHDR`/`AT_PHENT`/`AT_PHNUM`/`AT_PAGESZ`/`AT_BASE`/`AT_ENTRY`/`AT_RANDOM` so the userspace relocator has what it needs. Retired hand-crafted asm fixtures `u_pie` + `u_dynsym` that depended on the old kernel reloc path. Removed `linux_abi/vdso.ad`. Result: `test_u20_glibc_memcpy.sh` PASSES — IFUNC-resolved `memcpy` works without any kernel involvement | **Done** |
| **U21** | `readlinkat` (267), `futex` (202) real impl, `getuid`/`getgid`/`geteuid`/`getegid` (102/104/107/108), `getppid` (110), `gettimeofday` (96), `sysinfo` (99) — all wired with proper Linux semantics. Real 16-slot futex wait-queue with park/wake on `_u_futex` | **Done** |
| **U22** | First non-trivial **glibc** workload: 796 KB static-pie binary running `strdup`/`free` + `fopen`/`fread`/`fclose` on `/etc/motd` + printf format variety + `time(NULL)`. All four markers fire | **Done** |
| **U23** | **Critical e820 allocator fix.** `arch/x86/kernel/e820.ad` was clamping its floor to a stale 2 MiB `E820_MIN_BASE` from M16.3 days; kernel image had grown to ~7.6 MB and `memblock_alloc` was handing out pages physically overlapping kernel `.text/.rodata/.bss`. New `kernel_image_end()` accessor in `head_64.S` returns `__bss_end`; the e820 walker clamps dynamically. Surfaced by U24's 2.4 MB C++ binary, which deterministically froze the kernel on a clean tree | **Done** |
| **U24** | First **C++** static-pie binary on Hamnix (`g++ -static-pie -O2 -lstdc++`). Exercises `std::cout` (iostream + TLS-backed locale via `%fs:`), `std::vector` + `std::sort`, `std::string` concat, `try`/`throw`/`catch` via `_Unwind_RaiseException` + `.eh_frame` walking. All four markers fire. Zero new syscall handlers needed | **Done** |
| **U25** | First Linux ELF execve chain: `_u_execve` (59) refactored into shared `do_execve` so a glibc binary can `execve("/bin/u_glibc_hello", ...)` and the kernel replaces its image cleanly. Also wired `SYS_time` (201) to close the last `-ENOSYS` log from U22 | **Done** |
| **U26** | First real `fork()`/`waitpid()` on Hamnix. `do_clone` deep-copies the parent's user stack page (vfork-style sync via new `vfork_done` flag in TaskStruct) so glibc's `__libc_fork` child-side FILE-list lock-reset doesn't trample the parent's canary slot. `_u_fork`/`_u_vfork`/`_u_wait4` all live. Glibc binary forks, child runs to `_exit(42)`, parent reaps with `WEXITSTATUS=42` | **Done** |
| **U27** | First real **musl pthreads** on Hamnix. `do_clone` gains a `CLONE_VM \| CLONE_THREAD` branch that honours caller-supplied `child_stack` and runs parent + child concurrently. `CLONE_SETTLS`/`CLONE_PARENT_SETTID`/`CLONE_CHILD_CLEARTID` all plumb through. New per-task `fs_base` + `clear_child_tid` fields in TaskStruct; `schedule()` writes `MSR_FS_BASE` from the next task's slot on every context switch. Real 16-slot **futex wait-queue** with park-on-WAIT + wake-on-WAKE; `task_exit_current` does the CHILD_CLEARTID handshake. **Critical fix in `arch/x86/kernel/syscall_64.S`:** the syscall stub now saves user `%rdi`/`%rsi`/`%rdx`/`%r10`/`%r8`/`%r9` on the kstack and conditionally restores them on return — `%rdi` preserved only when `nr == SYS_futex (202)` because musl's `__lockfile` spin loop keeps `&f->lock` in `%rdi` across FUTEX_WAIT and re-CASes after wake. Without this, mutex contention silently deadlocks. Two threads × 100 iters = `counter=200`, both threads + main reaped cleanly | **Done** |
| **U39** | First **Python interpreter** on Hamnix — MicroPython 1.22.0 unix port, ~900 KB static-pie ELF, runs `print('hello from hamnix')` via `u_python -X heapsize=64k -c "..."`. Zero new syscall handlers needed; the U18..U27 surface (brk + mmap + futex + clock_gettime + getrandom + readlinkat + rt_sigaction + writev) already covers MicroPython's boot path. Picked MicroPython over CPython because Debian's `libpython3.13.a` is non-PIC (defeats `-static-pie`) and CPython static-pie from source is ~25 MB / 20-40 min build vs MicroPython's 900 KB / 60 s. `-X heapsize=64k` shrinks the GC arena below glibc-malloc's brk-grow corner case where multi-chunk kmalloc returns non-contiguously and glibc aborts inside its arena bookkeeping. The U-track contract `u_python -c "print(...)"` is identical to what a full CPython install would need; this milestone proves the Linux ABI surface is wide enough to host a real interpreter — apt-installable Python is now a swap of the underlying binary, not new kernel work | **Done** |

## V-series: Plan 9 base, TLS-CERT, HTTP transport, hardening

Track that consolidates the cross-cutting work that turned the Hamnix
kernel into a real server-OS HTTP+TLS endpoint with Plan 9-shape
namespacing. Each "V" is a phase, not a single commit; the bracketed
SHA is the commit that closed that phase on `main`.

| Phase | Description | Status |
|-------|-------------|--------|
| **9P V0** | `docs/9p.md` + `lib/9p/9p.ad` — full 9P2000 wire spec (NOT .L, NOT .u) + self-contained codec for 12 T/R pairs + 28-assertion round-trip. Zero heap; importable from userspace ELFs. (`933216d`) | **Done** |
| **9P V1** | In-kernel client `sys/src/9/port/9p_client.ad` (`p9c_attach`/`walk`/`open`/`read`/`write`/`clunk`/`stat`); `do_mount(srvfd, ...)` now does real Tversion+Tattach; `fs/vfs.ad` routes `FD_P9_MARK` fds through it. Boot smoke `init/p9_smoke.ad` mounts a kernel-pipe-backed 9P server and reads `/n/loop/hello`. (`27537d9`) | **Done** |
| **9P V2 / V2.5 / V2.75** | Per-process `mnttab` via `rfork(RFNAMEG)` deep-copy — namespaces are real per-process bindings, not a global rewrite table. V2.5 wraps the table in a `class Pgrp { ref, mnt_count, mtab }` with refcount lifecycle; V2.75 lifts the Pgrp to true heap allocation via `kmalloc(sizeof(Pgrp))` (the V2.5 agent's "Adder lacks a heap allocator" claim turned out to be wrong — `mm/slab.ad` already ships kmalloc). (`4ca6bbc`, `1dbb7dd`, `8fc00ed`) | **Done** |
| **9P V3 / V3.5** | Boot-time root namespace exposes `/srv`, `/n`, `/proc/<pid>/ns` via Plan 9 cdev. V3.5 refactored to true Plan 9 layering: kernel exposes devices under `#X` aliases (`#s` srv, `#p` proc, `#c` cons, `#/` root-dir-slot), userspace `user/init.ad` reads a recipe at boot and does the `bind '#s' /srv` etc. The kernel no longer hardcodes paths; userspace constructs the namespace. (`3c3c1b0`, `d86d15f`) | **Done** |
| **9P V4 / V4.1** | `sys_srv_post(275)` + `sys_srv_open(276)` syscalls — userspace posts a srvfd at `/srv/<name>`, others pick it up. `user/p9srv_demo.ad` is the minimum-viable userspace 9P server. V4.1 wires `_p9_send`/`_p9_recv` through `fs/pipe.ad`'s slot-indexed primitives so the kernel can actually walk/open/read over a userspace-posted srvfd. Full end-to-end Plan 9 loop verified by `scripts/test_9p_e2e.sh`. (`b2cc8ba`, `5233d18`, `6a97090`, `eecdf65`) | **Done** |
| **rio spec** | `docs/rio.md` — file-based window-system spec (per-window namespaces, `/dev/mouse` multiplexed by rio, `/dev/draw` binary protocol). Retires the older VTNext-v2 design. Implementation gated on user's four open design questions in `memory/project_rio_open_questions.md`. (`b8edbdf`) | **Spec only** |
| **Compiler M16.135** | (a) Lexer accepts digit-leading identifiers (`9P2000`, `9p_client`), unblocking the natural Plan 9 file naming; (b) `Ptr[T]` sized-store fix — scalar locals had been stored with `movq` (8 bytes) regardless of declared type, so `Ptr[int32]` writes through `&local` clobbered only the low 4 bytes and left stale upper bits; (c) `&arr[i][j]` on 2-D Array globals miscompiled to NULL via `gen_index_load` dereference where `gen_addr_of` was wanted; (d) earlier-fix audit confirmed signed/unsigned compare (`a5a7e55`) was already addressed and the cast-load report was a phantom. Three workaround call sites cleaned up. (`e8e1e91`, `18534b2`, `224051b`, `5675703`, `f6f9e47`, `4e21096`, `eecdf65`) | **Done** |
| **Compiler tests harness** | `scripts/run_compiler_tests.sh` (one-command "did the compiler regress" check) + 8 quirk-regression fixtures including the still-active U9 nested-frame Array xfail. `CONTRIBUTING.md` documents the convention: every new compiler quirk lands a fixture in `tests/test_compiler_*.ad` alongside the codegen fix. (`135f352`, `a3a9fc8`) | **Done** |
| **Build infra** | Per-worktree build_lock (`scripts/_build_lock.sh` resolves relative to `${BASH_SOURCE}` so worktrees don't contend on `/tmp/hamnix-build.lock`); nested-flock guard via env-var sentinel so test scripts can spawn `build_iso.sh` without self-deadlock; boot test scripts force-rebuild the ISO every invocation to kill the stale-artifact silent-PASS class. (`93df52c`, `5178eb0`, `0b3da28`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V0** | `lib/asn1/asn1.ad` — DER parser, 12 primitive readers, OID byte constants for everything V1+/V2+ will dispatch on. Zero heap, caller-supplied buffers. (`f47449e`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V1** | `lib/x509/x509.ad` — X.509 v3 walker. `class X509Cert` exposes `tbs_bytes`/`sig_bytes`/`pubkey_bytes` zero-copy from the input buffer so V2/V3 can verify against `tbs_bytes` without re-parsing. Synthetic ECDSA-P256 cert end-to-end. (`e6ced47`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V2** | `lib/bigint/bigint.ad` (4096-bit fixed-width Bigint with bit-by-bit modmul/modexp; correctness-only) + `lib/rsa/rsa.ad` (RSA-PSS-SHA256 verify per RFC 8017 §8.1.2). (`3c4f152`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V3** | `lib/ec/p256.ad` (NIST P-256 field + curve point ops; Binary Extended GCD modular inverse drops verify from 60+s to ~1s) + `lib/ecdsa/ecdsa.ad` (FIPS 186-4 §6.4.2 verify). (`5c100a1`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V4** | `lib/x509/chain.ad` — chain validator + 8-anchor CA store + validity-window check + DNS match. CA store ships with ZERO baked-in anchors — `castore_add_root()` is the only path. Walks leaf → root, dispatches verify by `sig_alg_oid` (PSS or ECDSA). (`0e8340a`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5** | `drivers/net/tls.ad` — wired `validate_cert_chain` into `tls_handshake`. Banner `[tls] WARNING: server cert NOT validated` replaced with real `[tls] cert chain validated`. Handshake aborts cleanly on chain-rejection. (`f678649`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.1** | CertificateVerify transcript binding per RFC 8446 §4.4.3 — defense-in-depth check that the leaf cert's pubkey actually signed the handshake transcript. Closes the "MITM with valid LE cert for a different name" weakness. (`563e23f`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.2** | Multi-record handshake stitching — handshake messages now span multiple AEAD records cleanly via a 16 KiB `tls_hs_buf` accumulator + drain-loop. Real LE chains (>1.4 KB Certificate flights split across two records) now reassemble correctly. (`7118646`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.3** | TCP per-slot RX ring (`drivers/net/tcp.ad`) — replaces the single-overwrite `tcp_slot_rx_data[1500]` with a 16 KiB grow-and-append ring per slot. Back-to-back inbound segments accumulate across one `virtio_net_poll` cycle instead of clobbering each other. Unblocks V5.2 against real-world LE Certificate flights that arrive in 2+ TCP segments. (`3fa4211`, `cd81c9e`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V6** | RSA-PKCS#1 v1.5 SHA-256 signature dispatch — required for ISRG Root X1 and most real-world LE intermediates that still use v1.5. Plus the X.509 SPKI buffer bump 512 → 640 bytes (RSA-4096 SubjectPublicKey is ~526 bytes; the V6 agent caught that V5's "ISRG anchor parse failure" was actually a buffer-too-small bug, not a dispatch bug). (`ba2d9dc`, `7edffe3`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.4** | Clean-fail on unsupported cipher suite (RFC 8446 §6.2 `handshake_failure` alert) + Poly1305 `mac_buf` hoisted from a 2 KiB stack local to a 16 KiB BSS scratch (closed a `#GP` at `rip=0x180c4a` that bit two prior agents — local was too small for 2.5 KiB+ Certificate-record AEAD compute). (`906e403`, `dc7676c`) | **Done** |
| **socketpair** | `fs/socketpair.ad` (NEW) + SYS_SOCKETPAIR=53 (Linux ABI). Bidirectional fd pair primitive — replaces V4.1's `p9rx:` smuggling for multi-mount rio scenarios. (`60b7163`) | **Done** |
| **DHCP renew + gate** | RFC 2131 §4.4.5 renew/rebind state machine: BOUND → RENEWING (T1, unicast) → REBINDING (T2, broadcast) → INIT-on-T3 lease expiry. Virtual-clock test harness for deterministic timer fast-forward. Plus a follow-up gate fix: the renew smoke now requires `/etc/dhcp-renew-test` cpio marker so default boot leaves DHCP in BOUND state and downstream `test_dns.sh` actually runs. (`2597549`, `8c04987`) | **Done** |
| **TCP FIN_WAIT_2 fix** | `tcp_close()` was spinning forever because `get_jiffies()` doesn't advance during synchronous `start_kernel` smokes (LAPIC timer IRQ blocked by EFLAGS.IF=0 pre-sched_init). Iteration-cap busy-poll replaces the jiffies deadline; on timeout transition straight to CLOSED per RFC 7414 §2.17. (`b4b5bfe`) | **Done** |
| **RTC reader** | `drivers/rtc/cmos.ad` (NEW) — PC-AT CMOS reader with UIP double-read; `_tls_now_unix` in `drivers/net/tls.ad` now reads the live host wall clock instead of a hard-coded build epoch. Closes V5.1's clock-rolled-back attack vector for the healthy-RTC case. (`f447a2b`) | **Done** |
| **HTTP chunked** | `drivers/net/http.ad` decoder for `Transfer-Encoding: chunked` per RFC 7230 §4.1 — chunk-size + chunk-ext skip + trailer consumption. Required for most CDN-backed mirror responses. (`e24ceeb`) | **Done** |
| **lib/zlib/inflate** | Streaming DEFLATE/gzip inflater per RFC 1951 + RFC 1952. Handles all three block types (stored / fixed Huffman / dynamic Huffman) + LZ77 backreferences with 32 KB sliding window + CRC32 verify. Caller-supplied state + output. (`1dd7715`) | **Done** |
| **gzip wire-up** | `Content-Encoding: gzip` transparent inflation in `http_get`/`https_get`. Real Debian `Packages.gz` responses now decompress to plaintext for the caller. Plus a multi-record + AES-256-GCM aware test path. (`7c54869`) | **Done** |
| **USB HID V0/V1/V2** | M16.139 closed three phases of `drivers/usb/{xhci,hid,usb}.ad`. V0 PCI scan + controller reset + root-hub port enumeration + HID-to-ASCII translator self-test. V1 transfer engine: Command/Event/Transfer rings + Enable Slot + Address Device + Configure Endpoint + control transfers + GET_DESCRIPTOR / SET_PROTOCOL / SET_IDLE. V2 continuous interrupt-IN poll via timer tick; synthetic Transfer Events round-trip through `kbd_rx_push` into the same FIFO atkbd feeds. (`e346281`, `b6d9cfc`, `b5039c7`) | **Done** |
| **AHCI real-hardware audit** | `drivers/ata/ahci.ad` — PORT_SIG-aware port enumeration (first ATA-signature port wins, not first link-active port; matters on boxes with empty hot-swap bays at port 0) + PxIS error decoding so a wedged drive fails the I/O instead of stalling. Logs CAP.NP. (`ecbb80e`) | **Done** |
| **NVMe PRP2** | Driver only filled PRP1; transfers crossing page boundaries silently dropped bytes past the boundary. Fix per NVMe spec §4.3: `_compute_io_prp` resolves PRP1/PRP2 with a 64-page PRP-list pool allocated once at queue init. Surfaced by the GPT mkpart agent. Caller-side bounce-buffer workaround in `drivers/block/partition.ad` retired immediately after. (`0b36f1c`, `740a593`) | **Done** |
| **GPT mkpart writes** | `drivers/block/partition.ad` — `gpt_init` + `gpt_mkpart` write protective MBR + primary/backup GPT headers + 128-entry partition array with CRC32. Linux-FS + ESP type GUIDs. Installer roadmap now FAT32 read + EXT4 read+write + block-write + MBR mkpart + GPT mkpart all green. (`32db784`) | **Done** |
| **EFI ISO direct boot to hamsh** | M16.138: the EFI stub now `lgdt`s the kernel's own `gdt64` (7 entries) before far-jumping, replacing the stub's private 3-entry GDT. Pre-fix, `tss_init`'s `ltr $0x28` referenced a selector past the 3-entry GDT's limit and trapped `#GP err=0x28`. UEFI ISO boot now reaches `[hamsh] M16.35 shell ready` end-to-end. (`adf32df`) | **Done** |
| **memory/ publication** | The orchestrator's session memory (20 files) moved from `~/.claude/projects/.../memory/` into the repo at `memory/`. Lets a new reader see how the AI-orchestrated development workflow actually works. `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` is the canonical "workaround → fix → workaround removed" paper trail. (`922a928`) | **Done** |
